<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>це<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ло<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***почва.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a> (3075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">подъшьва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podŭšĭva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sole (bottom); foundation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подошва.html>подо́шва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podóšva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sole, (mountain) foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póčva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чвы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чвы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>earth, soil, ground (mixture of sand and organic material)</li>
<li>basis, base, ground</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-почём-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***почему.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a> (119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of the preposition <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">according to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чему́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čemú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dative singular of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">počemú</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative adverb</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> why? <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">on what ground; according to what</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Počemú</b> vy govoríte éto?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Why do you say this?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́деть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Počemú</b> on želájet vídetʹ menjá?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Why does he wish to see me?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>For the answer, directly coordinate only with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potomú što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as well as with the solitary responses <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potomú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтому.html>поэ́тому</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poétomu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The literary <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ибо.html>и́бо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">íbo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> also fulfills a close role to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potomú što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">почему́-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">počemú-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***почерк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>по́черк</a> (4907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>по́черк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póčerk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>по́черка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>по́черки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>по́черков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>handwriting, hand (style of penmanship)</li>
<li><i>(individual manner of doing something)</i> hand, style</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>черк</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> разг. <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 3c(1): мн. ч. — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>почерка́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>почерко́в</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>почерка́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>почерка́ми</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>почерка́х</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:починенный.html>почи́ненный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">počínennyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:починок.html>почи́нок</a> (16605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:починок.html>почи́нок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">počínok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>

***почистить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почистить.html>почи́стить</a> (10222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čístitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почистить.html>почи́стить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">počístitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clean, to scour</li>
<li>to peel</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи́с<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тить</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a[②].      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-чист-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
